EVA: Efficient Reinforcement Learning for End-to-End Video Agent
Authors: Yaolun Zhang, Ruohui Wang, Jiahao Wang, Yepeng Tang, Xuanyu Zheng, Haonan Duan, Hao Lu, Hanming Deng, Lewei Lu
First: 2026-03-24T08:06:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T08:06:29+00:00
Comments: CVPR2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Video understanding with multimodal large language models (MLLMs) remains challenging due to the long token sequences of videos, which contain extensive temporal dependencies and redundant frames. Existing approaches typically treat MLLMs as passive recognizers, processing entire videos or uniformly sampled frames without adaptive reasoning. Recent agent-based methods introduce external tools, yet still depend on manually designed workflows and perception-first strategies, resulting in inefficiency on long videos. We present EVA, an Efficient Reinforcement Learning framework for End-to-End Video Agent, which enables planning-before-perception through iterative summary-plan-action-reflection reasoning. EVA autonomously decides what to watch, when to watch, and how to watch, achieving query-driven and efficient video understanding. To train such agents, we design a simple yet effective three-stage learning pipeline - comprising supervised fine-tuning (SFT), Kahneman-Tversky Optimization (KTO), and Generalized Reward Policy Optimization (GRPO) - that bridges supervised imitation and reinforcement learning. We further construct high-quality datasets for each stage, supporting stable and reproducible training. We evaluate EVA on six video understanding benchmarks, demonstrating its comprehensive capabilities. Compared with existing baselines, EVA achieves a substantial improvement of 6-12% over general MLLM baselines and a further 1-3% gain over prior adaptive agent methods. Our code and model are available at https://github.com/wangruohui/EfficientVideoAgent.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EVA：面向端到端视频智能体的高效强化学习框架
由于视频序列长、时序依赖复杂且存在冗余帧，基于多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的视频理解仍面临挑战。现有方法通常将MLLMs视为被动识别器，直接处理完整视频或均匀采样帧，缺乏自适应推理能力。近期基于智能体的方法虽引入外部工具，但仍依赖人工设计的工作流程和“先感知后决策”策略，导致长视频处理效率低下。本文提出EVA——一种面向端到端视频智能体的高效强化学习框架，通过迭代式的“摘要-规划-行动-反思”推理机制实现“先规划后感知”。EVA能自主决策观看内容、时机与方式，实现查询驱动的高效视频理解。为训练此类智能体，我们设计了一个简洁有效的三阶段学习流程：监督微调（SFT）、卡尼曼-特沃斯基优化（KTO）与广义奖励策略优化（GRPO），衔接监督模仿与强化学习。我们进一步构建了各阶段的高质量数据集，支持稳定可复现的训练。在六个视频理解基准测试中，EVA展现出全面能力：相比通用MLLM基线方法提升6-12%，较现有自适应智能体方法再提升1-3%。代码与模型已开源：https://github.com/wangruohui/EfficientVideoAgent。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency of existing multimodal large language models (MLLMs) and agent-based methods in processing long videos with redundant frames and static workflows, this paper introduces EVA, an efficient reinforcement learning framework for an end-to-end video agent. The method employs an iterative summary-plan-action-reflection reasoning process that enables query-driven, adaptive video understanding by deciding what, when, and how to watch, supported by a three-stage training pipeline combining supervised fine-tuning, Kahneman-Tversky Optimization, and Generalized Reward Policy Optimization. Experimental results on six benchmarks show that EVA outperforms general MLLM baselines by 6-12% and prior adaptive agent methods by an additional 1-3%, demonstrating comprehensive and efficient video understanding capabilities.
针对现有多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）和基于智能体的方法在处理长视频时存在冗余帧和静态工作流程导致的低效问题，本文提出了EVA，一种用于端到端视频智能体的高效强化学习框架。该方法采用迭代的总结-规划-行动-反思推理过程，通过自主决定观看内容、时机和方式来实现查询驱动的自适应视频理解，并辅以结合监督微调、卡尼曼-特沃斯基优化和广义奖励策略优化的三阶段训练流程。在六个基准测试上的实验结果表明，EVA相比通用MLLM基线性能提升6-12%，相比先前自适应智能体方法进一步提升1-3%，展现了全面且高效的视频理解能力。
Hybrid Stackelberg Game and Diffusion-based Auction for Two-tier Agentic AI Task Offloading in Internet of Agents
Authors: Yue Zhong, Yongju Tong, Jiawen Kang, Minghui Dai, Hong-Ning Dai, Zhou Su, Dusit Niyato
First: 2025-11-27T03:55:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T07:47:51+00:00
Comments: Revisions are needed
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The Internet of Agents (IoA) is rapidly gaining prominence as a foundational architecture for interconnected intelligent systems, designed to facilitate seamless discovery, communication, and collaborative reasoning among a vast network of Artificial Intelligence (AI) agents. Powered by Large Language and Vision-Language Models, IoA enables the development of interactive, rational agents capable of complex cooperation, moving far beyond traditional isolated models. IoA involves physical entities, i.e., Wireless Agents (WAs) with limited onboard resources, which need to offload their compute-intensive agentic AI services to nearby servers. Such servers can be Mobile Agents (MAs), e.g., vehicle agents, or Fixed Agents (FAs), e.g., end-side units agents. Given their fixed geographical locations and stable connectivity, FAs can serve as reliable communication gateways and task aggregation points. This stability allows them to effectively coordinate with and offload to an Aerial Agent (AA) tier, which has an advantage not affordable for highly mobile MAs with dynamic connectivity limitations. As such, we propose a two-tier optimization approach. The first tier employs a multi-leader multi-follower Stackelberg game. In the game, MAs and FAs act as the leaders who set resource prices. WAs are the followers to determine task offloading ratios. However, when FAs become overloaded, they can further offload tasks to available aerial resources. Therefore, the second tier introduces a Double Dutch Auction model where overloaded FAs act as the buyers to request resources, and AAs serve as the sellers for resource provision. We then develop a diffusion-based Deep Reinforcement Learning algorithm to solve the model. Numerical results demonstrate the superiority of our proposed scheme in facilitating task offloading.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于混合斯塔克尔伯格博弈与扩散拍卖的智能体互联网双层任务卸载机制
智能体互联网（IoA）作为互联智能系统的基础架构正迅速崛起，其通过大语言与视觉语言模型驱动，使智能体能够实现远超传统孤立模型的复杂协同交互。IoA中的无线智能体（WA）因本地资源有限，需将计算密集型AI服务卸载至邻近服务器——移动智能体（MA，如车载智能体）或固定智能体（FA，如边缘单元智能体）。FA凭借地理位置固定与连接稳定的特性，可作为可靠通信网关与任务聚合节点，并进一步协调卸载至具有动态连接优势的空中智能体（AA）层。为此，本文提出双层优化方案：第一层采用多领导者-多追随者斯塔克尔伯格博弈，由MA与FA作为领导者制定资源价格，WA作为追随者确定任务卸载比例；当FA过载时，第二层引入荷兰式双向拍卖模型，过载FA作为资源请求方，AA作为资源提供方。本文进一步开发基于扩散的深度强化学习算法求解模型，数值结果验证了所提方案在促进任务卸载方面的优越性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need for efficient task offloading in the Internet of Agents (IoA), where resource-constrained Wireless Agents (WAs) must offload compute-intensive AI services to nearby servers, such as Mobile Agents (MAs) or Fixed Agents (FAs), with FAs further able to offload to Aerial Agents (AAs) due to their stability. The method proposes a two-tier optimization: first, a multi-leader multi-follower Stackelberg game where MAs and FAs set resource prices and WAs determine offloading ratios; second, a Double Dutch Auction model for overloaded FAs to request resources from AAs, solved using a diffusion-based Deep Reinforcement Learning algorithm. Experimental results from numerical simulations demonstrate the scheme's superiority in facilitating effective task offloading within the IoA framework.
本文的动机是在智能体互联网（IoA）中实现高效的任务卸载，其中资源受限的无线智能体（WAs）需要将计算密集的AI服务卸载到附近的服务器，如移动智能体（MAs）或固定智能体（FAs），而FAs由于其稳定性可进一步卸载任务到空中智能体（AAs）。方法上提出了一种双层优化：第一层采用多领导者多跟随者的Stackelberg博弈，其中MAs和FAs设定资源价格，WAs决定卸载比例；第二层引入双荷兰拍卖模型，让过载的FAs作为买家向作为卖家的AAs请求资源，并通过基于扩散的深度强化学习算法求解模型。实验数值结果表明，该方案在促进IoA中的任务卸载方面具有优越性。
VLM-CAD: VLM-Optimized Collaborative Agent Design Workflow for Analog Circuit Sizing
Authors: Guanyuan Pan, Shuai Wang, Yugui Lin, Tiansheng Zhou, Pietro Liò, Zhenxin Zhao, Yaqi Wang
Venue: ACMMM 2026
First: 2026-01-12T08:37:32+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T07:44:42+00:00
Comments: submitted to the 34th ACM International Conference on Multimedia (ACMMM 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Vision Language Models (VLMs) have demonstrated remarkable potential in multimodal reasoning, yet they inherently suffer from spatial blindness and logical hallucinations when interpreting densely structured engineering content, such as analog circuit schematics. To address these challenges, we propose a Vision Language Model-Optimized Collaborative Agent Design Workflow for Analog Circuit Sizing (VLM-CAD) designed for robust, step-by-step reasoning over multimodal evidence. VLM-CAD bridges the modality gap by integrating a neuro-symbolic structural parsing module, Image2Net, which transforms raw pixels into explicit topological graphs and structured JSON representations to anchor VLM interpretation in deterministic facts. To ensure the reliability required for engineering decisions, we further propose ExTuRBO, an Explainable Trust Region Bayesian Optimization method. ExTuRBO serves as an explainable grounding engine, employing agent-generated semantic seeds to warm-start local searches and utilizing Automatic Relevance Determination to provide quantified evidence for the VLM's decisions. Experimental results on two complex circuit benchmarks demonstrate that VLM-CAD significantly enhances spatial reasoning accuracy and maintains physics-based explainability. VLM-CAD consistently satisfies complex specification requirements while achieving low power consumption, with a total runtime under 66 minutes, marking a significant step toward robust, explainable multimodal reasoning in specialized technical domains.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VLM-CAD：面向模拟电路尺寸优化的视觉语言模型协同智能体设计工作流
视觉语言模型在多模态推理中展现出显著潜力，但在解析模拟电路原理图等密集结构化工程内容时，存在固有的空间盲区与逻辑幻觉问题。为应对这些挑战，我们提出一种面向模拟电路尺寸优化的视觉语言模型协同智能体设计工作流，旨在实现基于多模态证据的鲁棒性分步推理。该工作流通过集成神经符号结构解析模块Image2Net来弥合模态鸿沟，该模块将原始像素转换为显式拓扑图与结构化JSON表示，从而将视觉语言模型解释锚定于确定性事实。为确保工程决策所需的可靠性，我们进一步提出可解释信任域贝叶斯优化方法，该方法作为可解释的 grounding 引擎，利用智能体生成的语义种子热启动局部搜索，并采用自动相关性判定为视觉语言模型决策提供量化证据。在两个复杂电路基准测试上的实验结果表明，该工作流显著提升了空间推理精度并保持基于物理解释性，在满足复杂规格要求的同时实现低功耗，总运行时间低于66分钟，标志着专业领域向鲁棒可解释多模态推理迈出重要一步。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitations of Vision Language Models (VLMs), such as spatial blindness and logical hallucinations, when interpreting complex analog circuit schematics, aiming to enable robust multimodal reasoning for engineering design. The proposed VLM-CAD method integrates a neuro-symbolic structural parsing module, Image2Net, to convert circuit images into topological graphs and structured JSON representations, and employs ExTuRBO, an explainable trust region Bayesian optimization method, to ground VLM decisions with semantic seeds and quantified evidence. Experiments on two circuit benchmarks show that VLM-CAD significantly improves spatial reasoning accuracy, maintains physics-based explainability, meets complex specifications with low power consumption, and completes tasks in under 66 minutes, advancing robust multimodal reasoning in technical domains.
本文针对视觉语言模型在解释复杂模拟电路原理图时存在的空间盲区和逻辑幻觉等局限性，旨在实现工程设计中稳健的多模态推理。所提出的VLM-CAD方法集成了一个神经符号结构解析模块Image2Net，将电路图像转换为拓扑图和结构化JSON表示，并采用可解释的信任域贝叶斯优化方法ExTuRBO，通过语义种子和量化证据来锚定VLM的决策。在两个电路基准测试上的实验结果表明，VLM-CAD显著提高了空间推理准确性，保持了基于物理的可解释性，在满足复杂规格要求的同时实现了低功耗，且总运行时间低于66分钟，推动了专业技术领域中稳健多模态推理的发展。
VLGOR: Visual-Language Knowledge Guided Offline Reinforcement Learning for Generalizable Agents
Authors: Pengsen Liu, Maosen Zeng, Nan Tang, Kaiyuan Li, Jing-Cheng Pang, Yunan Liu, Yang Yu
First: 2026-03-24T07:40:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T07:40:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Combining Large Language Models (LLMs) with Reinforcement Learning (RL) enables agents to interpret language instructions more effectively for task execution. However, LLMs typically lack direct perception of the physical environment, which limits their understanding of environmental dynamics and their ability to generalize to unseen tasks. To address this limitation, we propose Visual-Language Knowledge-Guided Offline Reinforcement Learning (VLGOR), a framework that integrates visual and language knowledge to generate imaginary rollouts, thereby enriching the interaction data. The core premise of VLGOR is to fine-tune a vision-language model to predict future states and actions conditioned on an initial visual observation and high-level instructions, ensuring that the generated rollouts remain temporally coherent and spatially plausible. Furthermore, we employ counterfactual prompts to produce more diverse rollouts for offline RL training, enabling the agent to acquire knowledge that facilitates following language instructions while grounding in environments based on visual cues. Experiments on robotic manipulation benchmarks demonstrate that VLGOR significantly improves performance on unseen tasks requiring novel optimal policies, achieving a success rate over 24% higher than the baseline methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：VLGOR：面向可泛化智能体的视觉-语言知识引导离线强化学习
将大语言模型与强化学习结合，可使智能体更有效地解析语言指令以执行任务。然而，大语言模型通常缺乏对物理环境的直接感知，这限制了其对环境动态的理解以及向未见任务泛化的能力。为突破此限制，我们提出视觉-语言知识引导离线强化学习框架，通过融合视觉与语言知识生成模拟交互轨迹，从而丰富交互数据。VLGOR的核心前提是微调视觉-语言模型，使其能基于初始视觉观测与高层级指令预测未来状态与动作，确保生成的轨迹保持时间连贯性与空间合理性。此外，我们采用反事实提示生成更多样化的轨迹用于离线强化学习训练，使智能体能够获取基于视觉线索理解环境、并遵循语言指令的知识。在机器人操作基准测试上的实验表明，VLGOR在需要新最优策略的未见任务上性能显著提升，成功率较基线方法提高超过24%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to enhance the generalization capabilities of agents in unseen tasks by addressing the limitation of Large Language Models (LLMs) in directly perceiving and understanding physical environments. The method introduces VLGOR, a framework that integrates visual and language knowledge to generate temporally coherent and spatially plausible imaginary rollouts, using a fine-tuned vision-language model conditioned on initial observations and instructions, along with counterfactual prompts to increase diversity. Main experimental results on robotic manipulation benchmarks show that VLGOR significantly outperforms baseline methods, achieving over a 24% higher success rate in tasks requiring novel optimal policies.
本研究的动机是通过解决大语言模型在直接感知和理解物理环境方面的局限性，来提升智能体在未见任务中的泛化能力。方法上提出了VLGOR框架，该框架整合视觉与语言知识，通过微调视觉语言模型，基于初始视觉观察和高级指令生成时间连贯且空间合理的想象轨迹，并利用反事实提示增加轨迹多样性以用于离线强化学习训练。主要实验结果表明，在机器人操作基准测试中，VLGOR在需要新最优策略的未见任务上表现显著优于基线方法，成功率提高了超过24%。
Grounding Sim-to-Real Generalization in Dexterous Manipulation: An Empirical Study with Vision-Language-Action Models
Authors: Ruixing Jin, Zicheng Zhu, Ruixiang Ouyang, Sheng Xu, Bo Yue, Zhizheng Wu, Guiliang Liu
First: 2026-03-24T07:21:29+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T07:21:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Learning a generalist control policy for dexterous manipulation typically relies on large-scale datasets. Given the high cost of real-world data collection, a practical alternative is to generate synthetic data through simulation. However, the resulting synthetic data often exhibits a significant gap from real-world distributions. While many prior studies have proposed algorithms to bridge the Sim-to-Real discrepancy, there remains a lack of principled research that grounds these methods in real-world manipulation tasks, particularly their performance on generalist policies such as Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models. In this study, we empirically examine the primary determinants of Sim-to-Real generalization across four dimensions: multi-level domain randomization, photorealistic rendering, physics-realistic modeling, and reinforcement learning updates. To support this study, we design a comprehensive evaluation protocol to quantify the real-world performance of manipulation tasks. The protocol accounts for key variations in background, lighting, distractors, object types, and spatial features. Through experiments involving over 10k real-world trials, we derive critical insights into Sim-to-Real transfer. To inform and advance future studies, we release both the robotic platforms and the evaluation protocol for public access to facilitate independent verification, thereby establishing a realistic and standardized benchmark for dexterous manipulation policies.
中文标题/摘要
标题：灵巧操作中仿真到现实泛化的实证研究：基于视觉-语言-动作模型
学习灵巧操作的通用控制策略通常依赖大规模数据集。鉴于真实世界数据采集成本高昂，一种实用替代方案是通过仿真生成合成数据。然而，合成数据常与现实世界分布存在显著差异。尽管已有许多研究提出算法以弥合仿真到现实的差异，但缺乏将这些方法扎根于真实操作任务的原则性研究，尤其是对视觉-语言-动作模型等通用策略的性能评估。本研究通过实证从四个维度检验仿真到现实泛化的关键决定因素：多层级域随机化、逼真渲染、物理真实建模及强化学习更新。为此，我们设计了综合评估协议以量化操作任务在现实世界的性能，涵盖背景、光照、干扰物、物体类型和空间特征等关键变量。通过超过一万次真实世界试验，我们得出仿真到现实迁移的重要结论。为促进未来研究，我们公开机器人平台与评估协议以供独立验证，从而为灵巧操作策略建立现实且标准化的基准。
Summary / 总结
This paper is motivated by the challenge of bridging the Sim-to-Real gap for training generalist dexterous manipulation policies, specifically Vision-Language-Action models, where real-world data is costly and synthetic data from simulation suffers from distributional discrepancies. The method involves an empirical study examining four key determinants of generalization: multi-level domain randomization, photorealistic rendering, physics-realistic modeling, and reinforcement learning updates, supported by a comprehensive evaluation protocol that accounts for variations in background, lighting, distractors, object types, and spatial features. The main experimental results, derived from over 10,000 real-world trials, provide critical insights into Sim-to-Real transfer, and the authors release the robotic platforms and evaluation protocol as a public benchmark to facilitate future research and verification.
本文的研究动机在于解决灵巧操作通用策略（特别是视觉-语言-动作模型）训练中的仿真到现实差距问题，因为真实世界数据收集成本高昂，而仿真生成的合成数据存在显著的分布差异。研究方法是对仿真到现实泛化的四个关键决定因素进行实证分析，包括多层级域随机化、逼真渲染、物理真实建模和强化学习更新，并设计了一个综合评估协议来量化操作任务在真实世界中的性能，该协议考虑了背景、光照、干扰物、物体类型和空间特征等关键变量。主要实验结果基于超过一万次真实世界试验，得出了关于仿真到现实迁移的重要见解，同时作者公开了机器人平台和评估协议，以建立一个现实且标准化的基准，促进未来研究和独立验证。
MJ1: Multimodal Judgment via Grounded Verification
Authors: Bhavesh Kumar, Dylan Feng, Leonard Tang
First: 2026-03-09T05:55:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T06:52:21+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multimodal judges struggle to ground decisions in visual evidence. We present MJ1, a multimodal judge trained with reinforcement learning that enforces visual grounding through a structured grounded verification chain (observations $\rightarrow$ claims $\rightarrow$ verification $\rightarrow$ evaluation $\rightarrow$ scoring) and a counterfactual consistency reward that penalizes position bias. Even without training, our mechanism improves base-model accuracy on MMRB2 by +3.8 points on Image Editing and +1.7 on Multimodal Reasoning. After training, MJ1, with only 3B active parameters, achieves 77.0% accuracy on MMRB2 and surpasses orders-of-magnitude larger models like Gemini-3-Pro. These results show that grounded verification and consistency-based training substantially improve multimodal judgment without increasing model scale.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MJ1：基于视觉验证的多模态判断模型
多模态判断模型常难以将决策基于视觉证据。我们提出MJ1，一种通过强化学习训练的多模态判断模型，采用结构化视觉验证链（观察→主张→验证→评估→评分）确保视觉依据，并通过反事实一致性奖励机制减少立场偏差。未经训练时，该机制在MMRB2基准上使基础模型在图像编辑任务准确率提升3.8点，多模态推理提升1.7点。训练后，仅含30亿激活参数的MJ1在MMRB2准确率达77.0%，超越Gemini-3-Pro等规模大数个量级的模型。结果表明，视觉验证与一致性训练能显著提升多模态判断能力，且无需扩大模型规模。

The paper addresses the issue that multimodal judges often fail to ground their decisions in visual evidence. CoMaTrack: Competitive Multi-Agent Game-Theoretic Tracking with Vision-Language-Action Models
Authors: Youzhi Liu, Li Gao, Liu Liu, Mingyang Lv, Yang Cai
First: 2026-03-24T06:35:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T06:35:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Embodied Visual Tracking (EVT), a core dynamic task in embodied intelligence, requires an agent to precisely follow a language-specified target. Yet most existing methods rely on single-agent imitation learning, suffering from costly expert data and limited generalization due to static training environments. Inspired by competition-driven capability evolution, we propose CoMaTrack, a competitive game-theoretic multi-agent reinforcement learning framework that trains agents in a dynamic adversarial setting with competitive subtasks, yielding stronger adaptive planning and interference-resilient strategies. We further introduce CoMaTrack-Bench, the first benchmark for competitive EVT, featuring game scenarios between a tracker and adaptive opponents across diverse environments and instructions, enabling standardized robustness evaluation under active adversarial interactions. Experiments show that CoMaTrack achieves state-of-the-art results on both standard benchmarks and CoMaTrack-Bench. Notably, a 3B VLM trained with our framework surpasses previous single-agent imitation learning methods based on 7B models on the challenging EVT-Bench, achieving 92.1% in STT, 74.2% in DT, and 57.5% in AT. The benchmark code will be available at https://github.com/wlqcode/CoMaTrack-Bench
中文标题/摘要

具身视觉追踪（EVT）作为具身智能的核心动态任务，要求智能体精准跟随语言指定的目标。然而现有方法多依赖单智能体模仿学习，受限于高成本专家数据与静态训练环境导致的泛化瓶颈。受竞争驱动能力演化的启发，我们提出CoMaTrack——一种基于博弈论的竞争性多智能体强化学习框架，通过在动态对抗环境中设置竞争性子任务训练智能体，形成更具适应性的规划能力与抗干扰策略。我们进一步构建首个竞争性EVT基准CoMaTrack-Bench，包含追踪器与自适应对手在多样化环境与指令下的博弈场景，支持主动对抗交互下的标准化鲁棒性评估。实验表明，CoMaTrack在标准基准与CoMaTrack-Bench上均达到最先进性能。值得注意的是，采用本框架训练的30亿参数视觉语言模型在挑战性EVT-Bench上超越此前基于70亿参数模型的单智能体模仿学习方法，在STT、DT、AT指标上分别达到92.1%、74.2%和57.5%。基准代码将发布于https://github.com/wlqcode/CoMaTrack-Bench

Motivated by the limitations of single-agent imitation learning in Embodied Visual Tracking (EVT), which suffers from expensive expert data and poor generalization, this paper introduces CoMaTrack, a competitive multi-agent reinforcement learning framework. The method employs a game-theoretic approach, training agents in adversarial settings with competitive subtasks to develop adaptive planning and interference-resilient strategies, and also presents CoMaTrack-Bench, a new benchmark for evaluating robustness in competitive EVT scenarios. Experimental results demonstrate state-of-the-art performance, where a 3B vision-language-action model trained with CoMaTrack outperforms prior 7B model-based single-agent methods on EVT-Bench, achieving scores of 92.1% in STT, 74.2% in DT, and 57.5% in AT.

A transformer architecture alteration to incentivise externalised reasoning
Authors: Elizabeth Pavlova, Mariia Koroliuk, Karthik Viswanathan, Cameron Tice, Edward James Young, Puria Radmard
First: 2026-03-22T19:28:21+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T06:21:38+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose a new architectural change, and post-training pipeline, for making LLMs more verbose reasoners by teaching a model to truncate forward passes early. We augment an existing transformer architecture with an early-exit mechanism at intermediate layers and train the model to exit at shallower layers when the next token can be predicted without deep computation. After a calibration stage, we incentivise the model to exit as early as possible while maintaining task performance using reinforcement learning. We provide preliminary results to this effect for small reasoning models, showing that they learn to adaptively reduce computations across tokens. We predict that, applied at the right scale, our approach can minimise the amount of excess computation that reasoning models have at their disposal to perform non-myopic planning using their internal activations, reserving this only for difficult-to-predict tokens.
中文标题/摘要
标题：一种激励外部化推理的Transformer架构改进方案

Improving Safety Alignment via Balanced Direct Preference Optimization
Authors: Shiji Zhao, Mengyang Wang, Shukun Xiong, Fangzhou Chen, Qihui Zhu, Shouwei Ruan, Yisong Xiao, Ranjie Duan, Xun Chen, XingXing Wei
First: 2026-03-24T06:04:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T06:04:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the rapid development and widespread application of Large Language Models (LLMs), their potential safety risks have attracted widespread attention. Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) has been adopted to enhance the safety performance of LLMs. As a simple and effective alternative to RLHF, Direct Preference Optimization (DPO) is widely used for safety alignment. However, safety alignment still suffers from severe overfitting, which limits its actual performance. This paper revisits the overfitting phenomenon from the perspective of the model's comprehension of the training data. We find that the Imbalanced Preference Comprehension phenomenon exists between responses in preference pairs, which compromises the model's safety performance. To address this, we propose Balanced Direct Preference Optimization (B-DPO), which adaptively modulates optimization strength between preferred and dispreferred responses based on mutual information. A series of experimental results show that B-DPO can enhance the safety capability while maintaining the competitive general capabilities of LLMs on various mainstream benchmarks compared to state-of-the-art methods. \color{red}{Warning: This paper contains examples of harmful texts, and reader discretion is recommended.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过平衡直接偏好优化提升安全对齐性能
随着大语言模型（LLMs）的快速发展和广泛应用，其潜在的安全风险已引起广泛关注。基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）被用于提升LLMs的安全性能。作为RLHF的一种简单有效替代方案，直接偏好优化（DPO）被广泛用于安全对齐。然而，安全对齐仍存在严重的过拟合问题，限制了其实际性能。本文从模型对训练数据的理解角度重新审视过拟合现象，发现偏好对中的响应之间存在不平衡偏好理解现象，这损害了模型的安全性能。为此，我们提出平衡直接偏好优化（B-DPO），基于互信息自适应调节偏好与非偏好响应间的优化强度。一系列实验结果表明，与前沿方法相比，B-DPO能在保持LLMs在主流基准测试中通用能力竞争力的同时，显著增强其安全性能。\color{red}{警告：本文包含有害文本示例，建议读者谨慎阅读。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the safety risks in large language models and the overfitting issues in existing safety alignment methods like Direct Preference Optimization (DPO), this paper identifies an Imbalanced Preference Comprehension phenomenon that hampers safety performance. The proposed method, Balanced Direct Preference Optimization (B-DPO), addresses this by adaptively adjusting optimization strength between preferred and dispreferred responses using mutual information. Experimental results demonstrate that B-DPO enhances safety capabilities while maintaining competitive general performance across various benchmarks compared to state-of-the-art methods.
本文针对大语言模型的安全风险以及直接偏好优化等方法在安全对齐中存在的过拟合问题，提出了模型对训练数据存在偏好理解不平衡现象，这损害了安全性能。为解决此问题，作者提出了平衡直接偏好优化方法，基于互信息自适应调节偏好与非偏好响应的优化强度。实验结果表明，与先进方法相比，该方法能在保持模型通用能力竞争力的同时，有效提升其在多种主流基准上的安全性能。
MemReward: Graph-Based Experience Memory for LLM Reward Prediction with Limited Labels
Authors: Tianyang Luo, Tao Feng, Zhigang Hua, Yan Xie, Shuang Yang, Ge Liu, Jiaxuan You
First: 2026-03-13T18:00:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T05:09:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in large language models (LLMs) have been driven by reinforcement-learning-based post-training, which requires multiple rollouts with rewards. However, obtaining ground truth labels for the calculation of rewards on a scale often requires expensive human labeling or time-consuming verification procedures. For instance, evaluating mathematical proofs demands expert review, and open-ended question answering lacks definitive ground truth. When ground truth labels are scarce, the effectiveness of reinforcement learning fine-tuning can be constrained. We introduce MemReward, a graph-based experience memory framework: an initial LLM policy generates rollouts for each query, each comprising a thinking process and a final answer, and these rollouts are stored as experience memory. Queries, thinking processes, and answers form nodes in a heterogeneous graph with similarity and structural edges; a GNN trained on labeled rollouts propagates rewards to unlabeled rollouts during online optimization. Experiments on Qwen2.5-3B and 1.5B in mathematics, question answering, and code generation demonstrate that MemReward, with only 20% labels, achieves 97.3% of Oracle performance on 3B and 96.6% on 1.5B, surpassing Oracle in out-of-domain tasks. Performance scales smoothly with label budget, reaching 99.4% of Oracle at 70% labels.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MemReward：基于图结构的经验记忆框架用于有限标注下的LLM奖励预测
大语言模型（LLM）的最新进展主要依赖于基于强化学习的后训练方法，该方法需要大量带奖励的轨迹数据。然而，大规模获取用于计算奖励的真实标注通常需要昂贵的人工标注或耗时的验证流程。例如，数学证明的评估需要专家评审，而开放式问答则缺乏明确的真实答案。当真实标注稀缺时，强化学习微调的效果会受到限制。本文提出MemReward，一种基于图结构的经验记忆框架：初始LLM策略为每个查询生成包含思维过程和最终答案的轨迹，这些轨迹被存储为经验记忆。查询、思维过程和答案构成异质图的节点，并通过相似性边和结构边连接；在在线优化过程中，基于标注轨迹训练的图神经网络（GNN）将奖励传播至未标注轨迹。在数学、问答和代码生成任务上对Qwen2.5-3B和1.5B模型的实验表明，MemReward仅使用20%的标注即可在3B模型上达到Oracle性能的97.3%，在1.5B模型上达到96.6%，并在跨域任务中超越Oracle性能。其性能随标注预算平滑提升，在70%标注时达到Oracle性能的99.4%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for MemReward stems from the high cost and scarcity of ground truth labels needed for reward calculation in reinforcement learning fine-tuning of large language models (LLMs). The method introduces a graph-based experience memory framework where an initial LLM generates rollouts for queries, which are stored as nodes in a heterogeneous graph; a Graph Neural Network (GNN) is then trained on a small set of labeled rollouts to propagate reward signals to unlabeled ones. Experimental results on Qwen2.5 models in mathematics, QA, and code generation show that with only 20% of labels, MemReward achieves 97.3% and 96.6% of Oracle performance for 3B and 1.5B models respectively, even surpassing Oracle in out-of-domain tasks, with performance scaling smoothly to 99.4% of Oracle at 70% labels.
MemReward的提出动机在于，大型语言模型（LLM）基于强化学习的后训练需要大量带奖励的轨迹，而获取用于计算奖励的真实标签通常成本高昂且稀缺。该方法采用了一种基于图的经验记忆框架：初始LLM策略为每个查询生成包含思维过程和最终答案的轨迹，并将其存储为经验记忆；查询、思维过程和答案构成异质图的节点，通过相似性和结构边连接；利用少量带标签轨迹训练的图神经网络（GNN）在在线优化过程中将奖励传播到未标记轨迹。在数学、问答和代码生成任务上对Qwen2.5-3B和1.5B模型的实验表明，仅使用20%的标签，MemReward即可分别达到Oracle性能的97.3%和96.6%，在跨域任务中甚至超越Oracle，且性能随标签预算平滑提升，在70%标签时达到Oracle的99.4%。
Almost Sure Convergence of Linear Temporal Difference Learning with Arbitrary Features
Authors: Jiuqi Wang, Shangtong Zhang
First: 2024-09-18T16:59:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T04:16:00+00:00
Comments: 36 pages, 0 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Temporal difference (TD) learning with linear function approximation (linear TD) is a classic and powerful prediction algorithm in reinforcement learning. While it is well-understood that linear TD converges almost surely to a unique point, this convergence traditionally requires the assumption that the features used by the approximator are linearly independent. However, this linear independence assumption does not hold in many practical scenarios. This work is the first to establish the almost sure convergence of linear TD without requiring linearly independent features. We prove that the weight iterates of linear TD converge to a bounded set, and that the value estimates derived from the weights in that set are the same almost everywhere. We also establish a notion of local stability of the weight iterates. Importantly, we do not impose assumptions tailored to feature dependence and do not modify the linear TD algorithm. Key to our analysis is a novel characterization of bounded invariant sets of the mean ODE of linear TD.
中文标题/摘要
标题：任意特征下线性时序差分学习的几乎必然收敛性
线性函数逼近的时序差分学习（线性TD）是强化学习中经典且强大的预测算法。尽管已知线性TD几乎必然收敛至唯一解，但传统收敛性分析要求逼近器所用特征线性无关。然而，该线性无关假设在许多实际场景中并不成立。本文首次在不要求特征线性无关的条件下，建立了线性TD的几乎必然收敛性。我们证明线性TD的权重迭代会收敛至一个有界集合，且从该集合中权重推导出的价值估计在几乎所有情况下均相同。我们还建立了权重迭代的局部稳定性概念。重要的是，我们未施加针对特征依赖性的特殊假设，也未修改线性TD算法。分析的关键在于对线性TD平均常微分方程有界不变集的新颖刻画。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the limitation of classic linear temporal difference (TD) learning, which traditionally requires linearly independent features for almost sure convergence, an assumption often violated in practice. The authors prove, for the first time, that linear TD converges almost surely even with arbitrary, potentially linearly dependent features, without modifying the algorithm or imposing tailored assumptions. Their analysis shows that the weight iterates converge to a bounded set where value estimates are consistent almost everywhere, and they establish local stability, relying on a novel characterization of bounded invariant sets for the associated mean ordinary differential equation.
本文针对经典线性时序差分学习通常需要特征线性独立才能确保几乎必然收敛的局限性展开研究，这一假设在实际中常不成立。作者首次证明了线性时序差分算法即使在使用任意、可能线性相关特征的情况下，也无需修改算法或附加特定假设，即可实现几乎必然收敛。分析表明权重迭代会收敛到一个有界集合，且该集合中的权重产生的值估计几乎处处一致，同时建立了局部稳定性，其关键在于对算法对应平均常微分方程有界不变集的新颖刻画。
FIPO: Eliciting Deep Reasoning with Future-KL Influenced Policy Optimization
Authors: Chiyu Ma, Shuo Yang, Kexin Huang, Jinda Lu, Haoming Meng, Shangshang Wang, Bolin Ding, Soroush Vosoughi, Guoyin Wang, Jingren Zhou
First: 2026-03-20T10:24:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T03:56:41+00:00
Comments: Switch links to offical websites
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present Future-KL Influenced Policy Optimization (FIPO), a reinforcement learning algorithm designed to overcome reasoning bottlenecks in large language models. While GRPO style training scales effectively, it typically relies on outcome-based rewards (ORM) that distribute a global advantage uniformly across every token in a trajectory. We argue that this coarse-grained credit assignment imposes a performance ceiling by failing to distinguish critical logical pivots from trivial tokens. FIPO addresses this by incorporating discounted future-KL divergence into the policy update, creating a dense advantage formulation that re-weights tokens based on their influence on subsequent trajectory behavior. Empirically, FIPO enables models to break through the length stagnation seen in standard baselines. Evaluated on Qwen2.5-32B, FIPO extends the average chain-of-thought length from roughly 4,000 to over 10,000 tokens and increases AIME 2024 Pass@1 accuracy from 50.0% to a peak of 58.0% (converging at approximately 56.0\%). This outperforms both DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Math-32B (around 47.0%) and o1-mini (approximately 56.0%). Our results suggest that establishing dense advantage formulations is a vital path for evolving ORM-based algorithms to unlock the full reasoning potential of base models. We open-source our training system, built on the verl framework.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FIPO：基于未来KL散度影响策略优化的深度推理激发方法
本文提出未来KL散度影响策略优化（FIPO），一种旨在突破大语言模型推理瓶颈的强化学习算法。虽然GRPO式训练能有效扩展，但其通常依赖基于结果的奖励模型（ORM），将全局优势均匀分配给轨迹中的每个词元。我们认为这种粗粒度的信用分配因未能区分关键逻辑支点与次要词元而形成了性能瓶颈。FIPO通过将折现后的未来KL散度纳入策略更新，构建了密集优势函数，根据词元对后续轨迹行为的影响重新分配权重。实验表明，FIPO使模型突破了标准基线的长度停滞现象。在Qwen2.5-32B上的评估显示，FIPO将平均思维链长度从约4000词元提升至超10000词元，并将AIME 2024 Pass@1准确率从50.0%提升至峰值58.0%（最终收敛于约56.0%），优于DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Math-32B（约47.0%）和o1-mini（约56.0%）。结果表明，建立密集优势函数是推动基于ORM的算法释放基础模型完整推理潜力的关键路径。我们开源了基于verl框架构建的训练系统。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Future-KL Influenced Policy Optimization (FIPO), a reinforcement learning algorithm motivated by the need to overcome reasoning bottlenecks in large language models, as standard outcome-based reward methods fail to provide fine-grained credit assignment for critical tokens. The method incorporates discounted future-KL divergence into policy updates to create a dense advantage formulation that re-weights tokens based on their influence on subsequent trajectory behavior. Experimental results on Qwen2.5-32B show that FIPO extends average chain-of-thought length from about 4,000 to over 10,000 tokens and increases AIME 2024 Pass@1 accuracy from 50.0% to a peak of 58.0%, outperforming baselines like DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Math-32B and matching or exceeding o1-mini.
本文提出了未来KL影响策略优化（FIPO），其动机是解决大语言模型中的推理瓶颈问题，因为标准基于结果的奖励方法无法对关键令牌进行细粒度信用分配。该方法将折扣后的未来KL散度纳入策略更新，创建密集优势公式，根据令牌对后续轨迹行为的影响重新加权。在Qwen2.5-32B上的实验结果表明，FIPO将平均思维链长度从约4000令牌扩展到超过10000令牌，并将AIME 2024 Pass@1准确率从50.0%提升至峰值58.0%，优于DeepSeek-R1-Zero-Math-32B等基线模型，并与o1-mini相当或更优。
Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro
Authors: KT Tech innovation Group
First: 2026-03-19T11:37:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T01:00:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The evolving LLM landscape requires capabilities beyond simple text generation, prioritizing multi-step reasoning, long-context understanding, and agentic workflows. This shift challenges existing models in enterprise environments, especially in Korean-language and domain-specific scenarios where scaling is insufficient. We introduce Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro, a 32B parameter flagship LLM designed to address enterprise-grade complexity through reasoning-focused optimization. Our methodology builds a robust data foundation via a quality-centric curation pipeline utilizing abstract syntax tree (AST) analysis for code, gap-filling synthesis for mathematics, and an LLM-based quality evaluator. Pre-training scales the model via layer-predictor-based Depth Upscaling (DuS) and a progressive strategy supporting a 128K token context window. Post-training introduces a specialized multi-stage pipeline, including Reasoning SFT, model merging, and asynchronous reinforcement learning (RL), to develop complex problem-solving skills. "Fusion Training" then rebalances these capabilities with conversational fluency, consistent response styling, and reliable tool-use. The evaluations show that Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro achieves competitive performance against leading global and domestic models. In addition, it sets state-of-the-art results on Korean-specific benchmarks, showcasing deep linguistic and cultural understanding. Finally, Responsible AI evaluations validate safety against attacks, ensuring a secure profile for deployment with a balance of harmlessness and responsiveness.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro
不断演进的大语言模型领域需要超越简单文本生成的能力，优先考虑多步推理、长上下文理解和智能体工作流。这一转变对企业环境中的现有模型构成挑战，尤其在韩语及特定领域场景中，现有模型的扩展能力不足。我们推出Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro，这是一款拥有320亿参数的旗舰大语言模型，通过以推理为核心的优化设计，旨在应对企业级复杂任务。 我们的方法通过以质量为中心的数据构建流程建立稳健的数据基础，包括：利用抽象语法树分析处理代码数据、通过填空合成增强数学能力，以及基于大语言模型的质量评估器。预训练阶段采用基于层预测器的深度上采样技术和渐进式策略扩展模型，支持128K词元的上下文窗口。后训练引入专门的多阶段流程，包括推理监督微调、模型融合和异步强化学习，以培养复杂问题解决能力。随后通过“融合训练”重新平衡这些能力与对话流畅性、一致的回答风格及可靠的工具使用。 评估显示，Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro在国内外领先模型中展现出竞争力，并在韩语专项基准测试中取得最先进成果，体现了深层的语言文化理解。最后，负责任人工智能评估验证了其抵御攻击的安全性，确保部署时兼具无害性与响应性的安全特性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for large language models that excel in multi-step reasoning, long-context tasks, and agentic workflows, particularly for Korean-language and enterprise applications, this work introduces Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro, a 32B parameter model. The method employs a quality-focused data pipeline using AST analysis and gap-filling, scales the model via Depth Upscaling for a 128K context window, and uses a specialized post-training pipeline including Reasoning SFT, model merging, and asynchronous RL, followed by Fusion Training for balanced capabilities. Experimental results demonstrate that the model achieves competitive performance against leading global and domestic models, sets state-of-the-art on Korean-specific benchmarks, and shows a secure, responsible AI profile in safety evaluations.
本研究旨在开发擅长多步推理、长上下文理解和智能体工作流的大语言模型，以应对韩语及企业级场景的特定需求，为此提出了拥有320亿参数的Mi:dm K 2.5 Pro模型。方法上，通过基于抽象语法树分析和填空合成的质量导向数据管道构建基础，采用深度扩展策略进行预训练以支持128K上下文窗口，并通过包含推理监督微调、模型融合和异步强化学习的专门后训练流程，最后进行融合训练以平衡各项技能。实验结果表明，该模型在国内外领先模型中具备竞争力，在韩语特定基准测试中取得了最优性能，并通过负责任人工智能评估验证了其安全性与可靠性。
Energy-Aware Reinforcement Learning for Robotic Manipulation of Articulated Components in Infrastructure Operation and Maintenance
Authors: Xiaowen Tao, Yinuo Wang, Haitao Ding, Yuanyang Qi, Ziyu Song
First: 2026-01-25T18:19:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-24T00:56:49+00:00
Comments: 18 pages, 5 figures, 7 tables. This version supersedes all previous preprint versions
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
With the growth of intelligent civil infrastructure and smart cities, operation and maintenance (O&M) increasingly requires safe, efficient, and energy-conscious robotic manipulation of articulated components, including access doors, service drawers, and pipeline valves. However, existing robotic approaches either focus primarily on grasping or target object-specific articulated manipulation, and they rarely incorporate explicit actuation energy into multi-objective optimisation, which limits their scalability and suitability for long-term deployment in real O&M settings. Therefore, this paper proposes an articulation-agnostic and energy-aware reinforcement learning framework for robotic manipulation in intelligent infrastructure O&M. The method combines part-guided 3D perception, weighted point sampling, and PointNet-based encoding to obtain a compact geometric representation that generalises across heterogeneous articulated objects. Manipulation is formulated as a Constrained Markov Decision Process (CMDP), in which actuation energy is explicitly modelled and regulated via a Lagrangian-based constrained Soft Actor-Critic scheme. The policy is trained end-to-end under this CMDP formulation, enabling effective articulated-object operation while satisfying a long-horizon energy budget. Experiments on representative O&M tasks demonstrate 16%-30% reductions in energy consumption, 16%-32% fewer steps to success, and consistently high success rates, indicating a scalable and sustainable solution for infrastructure O&M manipulation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向基础设施运维中关节部件机器人操控的能耗感知强化学习方法
随着智能民用基础设施与智慧城市的发展，运维作业日益需要安全、高效且能耗敏感的关节部件机器人操控技术，涉及检修门、服务抽屉、管道阀门等部件。然而现有机器人方法或侧重抓取操作，或针对特定关节对象，且鲜有将驱动能耗显式纳入多目标优化，限制了其在真实运维场景中长期部署的可扩展性与适用性。为此，本文提出一种面向智能基础设施运维的关节无关型能耗感知强化学习框架。该方法融合部件引导的三维感知、加权点采样及基于PointNet的编码技术，获得可泛化至异构关节对象的紧凑几何表征。操控任务被构建为约束马尔可夫决策过程，通过基于拉格朗日乘子的约束软演员-评论家方案对驱动能耗进行显式建模与调控。策略在此CMDP框架下进行端到端训练，在满足长期能耗预算的同时实现有效的关节对象操作。在典型运维任务上的实验表明，该方法可降低16%-30%的能耗，减少16%-32%的成功步数，并保持稳定的高成功率，为基础设施运维操控提供了可扩展且可持续的解决方案。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for safe, efficient, and energy-conscious robotic manipulation of diverse articulated components (like doors and valves) in smart city infrastructure operation and maintenance (O&M), this paper proposes an articulation-agnostic and energy-aware reinforcement learning framework. The method employs part-guided 3D perception and PointNet-based encoding for generalizable object representation and formulates manipulation as a Constrained Markov Decision Process (CMDP), explicitly regulating actuation energy via a Lagrangian-based constrained Soft Actor-Critic scheme. Experimental results on representative O&M tasks show the approach reduces energy consumption by 16%-30%, decreases the number of steps to success by 16%-32%, and maintains high success rates, demonstrating a scalable and sustainable solution.
本文的动机是智慧城市基础设施运维中需要对多种铰接部件（如检修门、阀门）进行安全、高效且节能的机器人操作。为此，论文提出了一种与具体铰接结构无关且具有节能意识的强化学习框架。该方法采用部件引导的3D感知和基于PointNet的编码来获得可泛化的物体几何表示，并将操作任务建模为一个约束马尔可夫决策过程，通过基于拉格朗日的约束Soft Actor-Critic方案来显式调控驱动能耗。在典型运维任务上的实验结果表明，该方法能降低16%-30%的能耗，减少16%-32%的成功所需步数，并保持高成功率，证明其是一个可扩展且可持续的解决方案。
Reinforcement-Guided Hyper-Heuristic Hyperparameter Optimization for Fair and Explainable Spiking Neural Network-Based Financial Fraud Detection
Authors: Sadman Mohammad Nasif, Md Abrar Jahin, M. F. Mridha
Venue: Knowledge-Based Systems (2026)
First: 2025-08-23T06:24:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T22:34:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The growing adoption of home banking systems has increased cyberfraud risks, requiring detection models that are accurate, fair, and explainable. While AI methods show promise, they face challenges including computational inefficiency, limited interpretability of spiking neural networks (SNNs), and instability in reinforcement learning (RL)-based hyperparameter optimization. We propose a framework combining a Cortical Spiking Network with Population Coding (CSNPC) and a Reinforcement-Guided Hyper-Heuristic Optimizer (RHOSS). CSNPC leverages population coding for robust classification, while RHOSS applies Q-learning to adaptively select low-level heuristics under fairness and recall constraints. Integrated within the MoSSTI framework, the system incorporates explainable AI via saliency maps and spike activity profiling. Evaluated on the Bank Account Fraud (BAF) dataset, the model achieves 90.8% recall at 5% false positive rate, outperforming prior spiking and classical models while maintaining over 98% predictive equality across demographic groups. Although RHOSS introduces offline optimization cost, it is amortized at deployment. The sparse architecture of CSNPC further reduces energy consumption compared to dense ANNs. Results demonstrate that combining population-coded SNNs with RL-guided hyper-heuristics enables fair, interpretable, and high-performance fraud detection.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化引导超启发式超参数优化的公平可解释脉冲神经网络金融欺诈检测
家庭银行系统的普及加剧了网络欺诈风险，需要兼具准确性、公平性与可解释性的检测模型。尽管人工智能方法展现出潜力，但仍面临计算效率低、脉冲神经网络（SNN）可解释性有限、以及基于强化学习（RL）的超参数优化不稳定等挑战。本研究提出一种融合皮层脉冲网络群体编码（CSNPC）与强化引导超启发式优化器（RHOSS）的框架。CSNPC利用群体编码实现鲁棒分类，RHOSS则通过Q学习在公平性与召回率约束下自适应选择底层启发式策略。该系统集成于MoSSTI框架中，通过显著性映射和脉冲活动分析实现可解释人工智能。在银行账户欺诈（BAF）数据集上的评估显示，该模型在5%误报率下达到90.8%召回率，优于现有脉冲模型与经典模型，同时在人口统计组间保持超过98%的预测公平性。尽管RHOSS引入离线优化成本，但可在部署阶段分摊。相比密集人工神经网络，CSNPC的稀疏架构进一步降低了能耗。结果表明：群体编码SNN与RL引导超启发式方法的结合，能够实现公平、可解释且高性能的欺诈检测。
Summary / 总结

The method introduces a framework combining a Cortical Spiking Network with Population Coding (CSNPC) for robust classification and a Reinforcement-Guided Hyper-Heuristic Optimizer (RHOSS) that uses Q-learning to adaptively tune hyperparameters under fairness and recall constraints, integrated with explainable AI techniques like saliency maps. Experimental results on the Bank Account Fraud dataset show the model achieves 90.8% recall at a 5% false positive rate, outperforming prior spiking and classical models, while maintaining over 98% predictive equality across demographic groups and reducing energy consumption through its sparse architecture.

Privacy-Preserving Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback via Decoupled Reward Modeling
Authors: Young Hyun Cho, Will Wei Sun
First: 2026-03-23T20:45:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-23T20:45:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Preference-based fine-tuning has become an important component in training large language models, and the data used at this stage may contain sensitive user information. A central question is how to design a differentially private pipeline that is well suited to the distinct structure of reinforcement learning from human feedback. We propose a privacy-preserving framework that imposes differential privacy only on reward learning and derives the final policy from the resulting private reward model. Theoretically, we study the suboptimality gap and show that privacy contributes an additional additive term beyond the usual non-private statistical error. We also establish a minimax lower bound and show that the dominant term changes with sample size and privacy level, which in turn characterizes regimes in which the upper bound is rate-optimal up to logarithmic factors. Empirically, synthetic experiments confirm the scaling predicted by the theory, and experiments on the Anthropic HH-RLHF dataset using the Gemma-2B-IT model show stronger private alignment performance than existing differentially private baseline methods across privacy budgets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于解耦奖励建模的隐私保护人类反馈强化学习
基于偏好的微调已成为训练大语言模型的重要环节，该阶段使用的数据可能包含敏感用户信息。核心问题在于如何设计适用于人类反馈强化学习独特结构的差分隐私流程。我们提出一种隐私保护框架，仅对奖励学习施加差分隐私约束，并从所得隐私奖励模型推导最终策略。理论上，我们分析了次优性差距，证明隐私约束会在常规非隐私统计误差之外引入附加项。同时建立了极小极大下界，表明主导项随样本量和隐私级别变化，从而刻画了上界在忽略对数因子时达到速率最优的区间。实证方面，合成实验验证了理论预测的标度关系；基于Gemma-2B-IT模型在Anthropic HH-RLHF数据集上的实验显示，本方法在各类隐私预算下均优于现有差分隐私基线方法的对齐性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to protect sensitive user data during preference-based fine-tuning of large language models, this paper introduces a privacy-preserving framework for reinforcement learning from human feedback that applies differential privacy exclusively to the reward modeling stage. The method decouples reward learning from policy derivation, theoretically analyzing the suboptimality gap to show that privacy introduces an additive error term beyond standard statistical errors, with minimax lower bounds indicating rate-optimality in certain regimes. Experimental results on synthetic data align with theoretical predictions, and tests using the Anthropic HH-RLHF dataset with the Gemma-2B-IT model demonstrate superior alignment performance over existing differentially private baselines across various privacy budgets.
针对大型语言模型基于偏好的微调过程中可能涉及敏感用户数据的问题，本文提出了一种保护隐私的人类反馈强化学习框架，其核心方法是将差分隐私仅应用于奖励建模阶段，而与策略推导过程解耦。理论分析表明，隐私保护会在常规统计误差之外引入一个附加的次优性差距项，并通过极小极大下界证明了在某些样本量与隐私水平下，其上界在忽略对数因子后是速率最优的。在合成数据上的实验验证了理论预测的缩放规律，同时基于Anthropic HH-RLHF数据集和Gemma-2B-IT模型的实验显示，该方法在不同隐私预算下均优于现有的差分隐私基线方法，实现了更强的私有对齐性能。
